  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.101124s; animation-duration: 0.8s;" class="preFade fadeIn">Prisms Data Privacy Policy</h2><p class="preFade fadeIn" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.106742s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.11236s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">Last Updated: June 24, 2021</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.117978s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">Prisms of Reality, Inc. (“<strong>Prisms</strong>,” the “Company,” “we,” or “us”) is transforming math education to provide a more immersive and effective learning experience through virtual reality. This Privacy Policy is designed to help you understand how we collect, use, and share your personal information and to help you understand and exercise your privacy rights. Your privacy is very important to us and we are committed to protecting it.</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.123596s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">1.	SCOPE</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.129213s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">2.	PERSONAL INFORMATION WE COLLECT</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.134831s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">3.	HOW WE USE YOUR INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.140449s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">4.	HOW WE DISCLOSE YOUR INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.146067s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">5.	YOUR PRIVACY CHOICES AND RIGHTS</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.151685s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">6.	SECURITY OF YOUR INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.157303s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">7.	INTERNATIONAL DATA TRANSFERS</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.162921s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">8.	RETENTION OF PERSONAL INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.168539s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">9.	SUPPLEMENTAL NOTICE FOR CALIFORNIA RESIDENTS</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.174157s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">10.	SUPPLEMENTAL NOTICE FOR NEVADA RESIDENTS</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.179775s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">11.	CHILDREN’S INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.185393s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">12.	OTHER PROVISIONS</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.191011s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">13.	CONTACT US</p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.196629s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.202247s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>1. SCOPE</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.207865s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">This Privacy Policy applies to personal information processed by us, including on our websites, mobile applications, and other online or offline offerings. To make this Privacy Policy easier to read, our websites, mobile applications, and other offerings are collectively called “<strong>Services.</strong>”</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.213483s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">This Privacy Policy does not apply to any of the personal information that our educational system customers may collect and process using Prisms’ Services (“Customer Data”). Our customers’ respective privacy policies govern their collection and use of Customer Data. Our processing of Customer Data is governed by the contracts that we have in place with our customers, not this Privacy Policy. Any questions or requests relating to Customer Data should be directed to our customer.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.219101s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>2. PERSONAL INFORMATION WE COLLECT</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.224719s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">The categories of personal information we collect depend on how you interact with us, our Services, and the requirements of applicable law. We collect information that you provide to us, information we obtain automatically when you use our Services, and information from other sources such as third-party services and organizations, as described below.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.230337s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>        A. Information You Provide to Us Directly</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.235955s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">We may collect the following personal information that you provide to us.</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.241573s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Account Creation</strong>. We may collect information when you create an account, such as name, email address, and password.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.247191s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Your Communications with Us</strong>. We may collect personal information, such as name, email address, and phone number when you request information about our Services, request customer or technical support, apply for a job, or otherwise communicate with us.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.252809s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Surveys</strong>. We may contact you to participate in surveys. If you decide to participate, you may be asked to provide certain information which may include personal information.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.258427s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Sweepstakes or Contests</strong>. We may collect personal information you provide for any sweepstakes or contests that we offer. In some jurisdictions, we are required to publicly share information of sweepstakes and contest winners.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.264045s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Conferences, Trade Shows, and Other Events.</strong> We may collect personal information from individuals when we attend conferences, trade shows, and other events.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.269663s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Business Development and Strategic Partnerships.</strong> We may collect personal information from individuals and third parties to assess and pursue potential business opportunities.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.275281s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Job Applications.</strong> We may post job openings and opportunities on our Services. If you reply to one of these postings by submitting your application, CV and/or cover letter to us, we will collect and use your information to assess your qualifications.</p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.280899s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.286517s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>B. Information Collected Automatically</strong></p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.292135s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">We may collect personal information automatically when you use our Services:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.297753s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Service Information</strong>. We record user activity during the learning experience in our modules. We use anonymous user ID codes to aggregate and categorize the data we collect. Our data logging captures information such as:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.303371s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">Timestamps of when recorded activities occur;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.308989s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">3D tool usage and metrics (e.g., duration, frequency);</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.314607s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">Formative assessment data (e.g., answer submissions to in module questions);</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.320225s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">Objects that are visible to the user’s viewport at a given time (i.e., what objects the user is looking at);</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.325843s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">Hints provided by the virtual system; and</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.331461s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">Any errors or software crashes.</p></li></ul></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.337079s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Device and Network Information</strong>. We may collect certain information automatically when you use our Services, such as your Internet protocol (IP) address, user settings, MAC address, cookie identifiers, mobile carrier, mobile advertising and other unique identifiers, browser or device information, location information (including approximate location derived from IP address), and Internet service provider. We may also automatically collect other information regarding your use of our Services, such as pages that you visit before, during and after using our Services, information about the links you click, the types of content you interact with, the frequency and duration of your activities, and other information about how you use our Services.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.342697s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Cookies, Pixel Tags/Web Beacons, and Other Technologies</strong>. We, as well as third parties that provide content, advertising, or other functionality on our Services, may use cookies, pixel tags, local storage, and other technologies (“<strong>Technologies</strong>”) to automatically collect information through your use of our Services.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.348315s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Cookies</strong>. Cookies are small text files placed in device browsers that store preferences and facilitate and enhance your experience.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.353933s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Pixel Tags/Web Beacons</strong>. A pixel tag (also known as a web beacon) is a piece of code embedded in our Services that collects information about engagement on our Services. The use of a pixel tag allows us to record, for example, that a user has visited a particular web page or clicked on a particular advertisement. We may also include web beacons in e-mails to understand whether messages have been opened, acted on, or forwarded.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.359551s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">Our uses of these Technologies fall into the following general categories:&nbsp;</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.365169s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Operationally Necessary</strong>. This includes Technologies that allow you access to our Services, applications, and tools that are required to identify irregular website behavior, prevent fraudulent activity and improve security or that allow you to make use of our functionality;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.370787s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Performance-Related</strong>. We may use Technologies to assess the performance of our Services, including as part of our analytic practices to help us understand how individuals use our Services (<em>see Analytics below</em>);</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.376404s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Functionality-Related</strong>. We may use Technologies that allow us to offer you enhanced functionality when accessing or using our Services. This may include identifying you when you sign into our Services or keeping track of your specified preferences, interests, or past items viewed;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.382022s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Advertising- or Targeting-Related</strong>. We may use first party or third-party Technologies to deliver content, including ads relevant to your interests, on our Services or on third-party websites.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.38764s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><em>See “Your Privacy Choices and Rights” below to understand your choices regarding these Technologies.</em></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.393258s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Analytics</strong>. We may use Technologies and other third-party tools to process analytics information on our Services. For example, our analytics partners include Google Analytics. For more information, please visit <a href="http://www.google.com/policies/privacy/partners/"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Google Analytics’ Privacy Policy</span></a>. To learn more about how to opt-out of Google Analytics’ use of your information, please click <a href="http://tools.google.com/dlpage/gaoptout"><span style="text-decoration:underline">here</span></a>.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.398876s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>C. Information Collected from Other Sources</strong></p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.404494s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">We may obtain information about you from other sources, including through third-party services and organizations, including our customers. For example, if you access our Services through a third-party application, such as an app store, a third-party login service, or a social networking site, we may collect information about you from that third-party application that you have made available via your privacy settings.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.410112s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>3. HOW WE USE YOUR INFORMATION</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.41573s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">We use your information for a variety of business purposes, including to provide our Services, for administrative purposes, and to market our products and Services, as described below.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.421348s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>     A. transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.47191s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">Allowing you to register for events.<br></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; Administrative Purposes</strong></p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.483146s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">We use your information for various administrative purposes, such as:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; We do not use the personal information of children for marketing purposes. We may provide you with these materials as permitted by applicable law.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.58427s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">If you have any questions about our marketing practices or if you would like to opt out of the use of your personal information for marketing purposes, you may contact us at any time as set forth in “Contact Us” below.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.589888s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>     D. Other Purposes</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.595506s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">We also use your information for other purposes as requested by you or as permitted by applicable law.</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.601124s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Consent</strong>. We may use personal information for other purposes that are clearly disclosed to you at the time you provide personal information or with your consent.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.606742s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>De-identified and Aggregated Information</strong>. We may use personal information and other information about you to create de-identified and/or aggregated information, such as de-identified demographic information, de-identified location information, information about the device from which you access our Services, or other analyses we create.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.61236s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>4. This includes service providers that provide us with IT support, hosting, software installation on the VR headsets, customer service, and related services.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.640449s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>APIs/SDKs</strong>. YOUR PRIVACY CHOICES AND RIGHTS</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.679775s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Your Privacy Choices</strong>. The privacy choices you may have about your personal information are determined by applicable law and are described below.&nbsp;</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.685393s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Email and Telephone Communications</strong>. If you receive an unwanted email from us, you can use the unsubscribe link found at the bottom of the email to opt out of receiving future emails. Note that you will continue to receive transaction-related emails regarding products or Services you have requested. We may also send you certain non-promotional communications regarding us and our Services, and you will not be able to opt out of those communications (e.g., communications regarding our Services or updates to our Terms or this Privacy Policy).</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.691011s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">We process requests to be placed on do-not-mail, do-not-phone, and do-not-contact lists as required by applicable law.</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.696629s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Mobile Devices</strong>. We may send you push notifications through our mobile application. You may opt out from receiving these push notifications by changing the settings on your mobile device. With your consent, we may also collect precise location-based information via our mobile application. You may opt out of this collection by changing the settings on your mobile device.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.702247s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>“Do Not Track</strong>.<strong>”</strong> Do Not Track (“DNT”) is a privacy preference that users can set in certain web browsers. Please note that we do not respond to or honor DNT signals or similar mechanisms transmitted by web browsers.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.707865s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Cookies and Interest-Based Advertising</strong>. You may stop or restrict the placement of Technologies on your device or remove them by adjusting your preferences as your browser or device permits. However, if you adjust your preferences, our Services may not work properly. Please note that cookie-based opt-outs are not effective on mobile applications. However, you may opt-out of personalized advertisements on some mobile applications by following the instructions for <a href="https://support.google.com/googleplay/android-developer/answer/6048248?hl=en"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Android</span></a>, <a href="https://support.apple.com/en-us/HT202074"><span style="text-decoration:underline">iOS</span></a> and <a href="https://www.networkadvertising.org/mobile-choice/"><span style="text-decoration:underline">others</span></a>.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.713483s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">The online advertising industry also provides websites from which you may opt out of receiving targeted ads from data partners and other advertising partners that participate in self-regulatory programs. You can access these and learn more about targeted advertising and consumer choice and privacy by visiting the <a href="http://www.networkadvertising.org/managing/opt_out.asp"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Network Advertising Initiative</span></a> and <a href="http://www.aboutads.info/choices/"><span style="text-decoration:underline">the Digital Advertising Alliance</span></a>. &nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.719101s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">Please note you must separately opt out in each browser and on each device.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.724719s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Your Privacy Rights</strong>. We will process such requests in accordance with applicable laws.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.764045s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>6. SECURITY OF YOUR INFORMATION</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.769663s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">We take steps to ensure that your information is treated securely and in accordance with this Privacy Policy.<em> </em>Unfortunately, no system is 100% secure, and we cannot ensure or warrant the security of any information you provide to us. We endeavor to safeguard your information consistent with the requirements of applicable laws.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.792135s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>8. You may also make a verifiable consumer request on behalf of your minor child. To designate an authorized agent, please contact us as set forth in “Contact Us” below.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.837079s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Verification</strong>. To protect your privacy, we may need to verify your identity before fulfilling your privacy request. To conduct such verification, we will ask you to provide sufficient information that allows us to reasonably verify you are the person about whom we collected personal information or an authorized representative, which may include asking you to answer questions regarding your account and use of our Services.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.842697s; animation-duration: 0.8s;">If you are a California resident and would like to exercise any of your privacy rights, please contact us as set forth in “Contact Us” below. We will process such requests in accordance with applicable laws.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.848315s; animation-duration: 0.8s;"><strong>Accessibility</strong>.
